TAMIL NADU STATE ELECTION COMMISSION, CHENNAI
[ELECTIONS—ORDINARY ELECTIONS TO RURAL LOCAL BODIES—OCTOBER 2011-VELLORE DISTRICT-CONTESTED
CANDIDATES—ACCOUNTS OF ELECTION EXPENSES—FAILURE TO LODGE—SHOW CAUSE NOTICES ISSUED —
DISQUALIFICATION—ORDERED.]
(S.O. No.37/2013/TNSEC/PE-2.)
NO. VI(2)/213(b-1)/2013.
WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. first read above, by invoking sub-rule (3) of the rule 120
of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats (Elections) Rules, 1995, the Commission directed that all the contesting candidates
in the elections listed therein shall lodge a true copy of their election expenses kept by them or by their respective
election agent under sub-rule (1) of rule 120 of the said Rules in the format prescribed there for under sub-rule (2)
of the rule 120 of the said Rules with the officers mentioned therein, within thirty days from the date of declaration
of the result of the elections;
2.  WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. second read above, this Commission prescribed
a format for the said purpose by invoking sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules;
3.  WHEREAS, this Commission conducted Ordinary Elections to the Rural Local Bodies during October
2011;
4.  WHEREAS, the District Election Officer/District Collector, Vellore, in the letter third read above reported
that 906 candidates contested in the said Ordinary Elections for various offices  failed to lodge copies of their
account of election expenses as directed by this Commission;
5.  WHEREAS, based on the report of the said District Election Officer/District Collector, a show cause
notice was issued   in the reference fourth read above to each of the contested candidate who failed to lodge a
true copy of the account of election expenses in the Ordinary Elections held during the month of October, 2011,
through the District Election Officer/District Collector, calling for explanation within 20 days of the receipt of the said
Notice, as to why action should not be taken against him/her as per sub-section (4) of section 37 of the Tamil Nadu
Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994);
DTP—VI-2 Ex. (300)—1
[ 1 ]


                      TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
2 
6.  WHEREAS, on receipt of show cause notice 19 number of candidates have submitted their 
account directly to the Commission and the same have been forwarded to District Election Officer in the 
reference sixth cited and requested to send his remarks along with the reports of other candidates. 
 
 
7.  WHEREAS, the said District Election Officer/District Collector, in his letter seventh  read above, 
has now reported that out of the said 906 contested candidates three of them have expired, 305 contested 
candidates have submitted their explanation along with the accounts within the time prescibed and 598 
contested candidates, have neither submitted their explanations nor  lodged the account of election 
expenses in spite of the show cause notices issued to them; and 
 
 
8.  WHEREAS, in view of the said report of the District Election Officer/District Collector, the  
Tamil Nadu State Election Commission is satisfied that 598 candidates listed in column (3) of the Table 
below against the contested election mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, have failed 
to lodge an account of election expenses as required by or under the said Act and have no justification for 
the failure. 
 
 
9.  NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (4) of section 37 of the 
Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994), the Tamil Nadu State Election Commission 
hereby declares that the candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below against the contested election 
mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, shall be disqualified, for being chosen as a 
member or president for a period of three years from the date of this Order.

[ELECTIONS – ORDINARY ELECTIONS TO RURAL LOCAL BODIES – OCTOBER 2011 – 
DHARMAPURI DISTRICT – CONTESTED CANDIDATES – ACCOUNTS OF ELECTION 
EXPENSES  - FAILURE TO LODGE - SHOW CAUSE NOTICES ISSUED – FAILED TO SUBMIT 
EXPLANATION AND ACCOUNTS DISQUALIFICATION – ORDERED.] 
 
(S.O.No.38/2013/TNSEC/PE-2.)                         
 
NO. VI (2)/ 213(b-2) /2013. 
 
WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. first read above, by invoking sub-rule (3) of the 
rule 120 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats (Elections) Rules, 1995, the Commission directed that all the 
contesting candidates in the elections listed therein shall lodge a true copy of their election expenses kept by 
them or by their respective election agent under sub-rule (1) of rule 120 of the said Rules in the format 
prescribed therefor under sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules with the officers mentioned therein, 
within thirty days from the date of declaration of the result of the elections; 
 
 
2. WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. second read above, this Commission 
prescribed a format for the said purpose by invoking sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules; 
 
 
3.  WHEREAS, this Commission conducted Ordinary Elections to the Rural Local Bodies during 
October 2011; 
 
 
4.  WHEREAS, the District Election Officer/District Collector, Dharmapuri, in the letter third read 
above reported that 770 candidates contested in the said Ordinary Elections for various offices failed to 
lodge copies of their account of election expenses as directed by this Commission; 
 
 
5. WHEREAS, based on the report of the said District Election Officer/District Collector, a show 
cause notice was issued   in the reference fourth read above to each of the contested candidate who failed to 
lodge a true copy of the account of election expenses in the Ordinary Elections held during the month of 
October, 2011, through the District Election Officer/District Collector, calling for explanation within 20 days of 
the receipt of the said Notice, as to why action should not be taken against him/her as per sub-section (4) of 
section 37 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994); 
 
6.  WHEREAS, on receipt of show cause notices 14 number of candidates have submitted their 
account directly to the Commission and the same have been forwarded to District Election Officer in the 
reference sixth cited and requested to send his remarks along with the reports of other candidates. 
 
7. WHEREAS, the said District Election Officer/District Collector, in his letter seventh read above, 
has now reported that out of the said 770 contested candidates two of them have expired, 136 contested 
candidates have submitted their explanation along with the accounts within the time prescibed and                    
632 contested candidates, have neither submitted their explanations nor lodged the account of election 
expenses in spite of the show cause notices issued to them; and 


                      TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
58 
 8. WHEREAS, in view of the said report of the District Election Officer/District Collector, the              
Tamil Nadu State Election Commission is satisfied that 632 candidates listed in column (3) of the Table 
below against the contested election mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, have failed 
to lodge an account of election expenses as required by or under the said Act and have no justification for 
the failure. 
 
 
9.   NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (4) of section 37 of the 
Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994), the Tamil Nadu State Election Commission 
hereby declares that the candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below against the contested election 
mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, shall be disqualified, for being chosen as a 
member or president for a period of three years from the date of this Order.

                      TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
104 
  
 
[ELECTIONS – ORDINARY ELECTIONS TO RURAL LOCAL BODIES – OCTOBER 2011 – 
TIRUVALLUR  DISTRICT – CONTESTED CANDIDATES – ACCOUNTS OF ELECTION 
EXPENSES  - FAILURE TO LODGE - SHOW CAUSE NOTICES ISSUED – FAILED TO 
SUBMIT EXPLANATION AND ACCOUNTS - DISQUALIFICATION – ORDERED.] 
 
(S.O.No.39/2013/TNSEC/PE-2.)  
 
NO. VI (2)/213(b-3) /2013. 
 
 
 
WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. first read above, by invoking sub-rule (3) of the 
rule 120 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats (Elections) Rules, 1995, the Commission directed that all the 
contesting candidates in the elections listed therein shall lodge a true copy of their election expenses kept by 
them or by their respective election agent under sub-rule (1) of rule 120 of the said Rules in the format 
prescribed therefor under sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules with the officers mentioned therein, 
within thirty days from the date of declaration of the result of the elections; 
 
 
2.  WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. second read above, this Commission 
prescribed a format for the said purpose by invoking sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules; 
 
 
3.   WHEREAS, this Commission conducted Ordinary Elections to the Rural Local Bodies during 
October 2011; 
 
 
4.  WHEREAS, the District Election Officer/District Collector, Tiruvallur, in the letter third read above 
reported that 1267 candidates contested in the said Ordinary Elections for various offices  failed to lodge 
copies of their account of election expenses as directed by this Commission; 
 
 
5.   WHEREAS, based on the report of the said District Election Officer/District Collector, a show 
cause notice was issued   in the reference fourth read above to each of the contested candidate who failed to 
lodge a true copy of the account of election expenses in the Ordinary Elections held during the month of 
October, 2011, through the District Election Officer/District Collector, calling for explanation within 20 days of 
the receipt of the said Notice, as to why action should not be taken against him/her as per sub-section (4) of 
section 37 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994); 
 
6.   WHEREAS, on receipt of show cause notices 59 number of candidates have submitted their 
account directly to the Commission and the same have been forwarded to District Election Officer in the 
reference sixth cited and requested to send his remarks along with the reports of other candidates. 
 
 
7.   WHEREAS, the said District Election Officer/District Collector, in his letter seventh read above, 
has now reported that out of the said 1267 contested candidates  four  of them have expired, 368  contested 
candidates have submitted their explanation along with the accounts within the time prescibed and                    
629. 
Village Panchayat President,

                         TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY                 105
 
895 contested candidates, have neither submitted their explanations nor  lodged the account of election 
expenses in spite of the show cause notices issued to them; and 
 
 
8.   WHEREAS, in view of the said report of the District Election Officer/District Collector, the           
Tamil Nadu State Election Commission is satisfied that 895 candidates listed in column (3) of the Table 
below against the contested election mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, have failed 
to lodge an account of election expenses as required by or under the said Act and have no justification for 
the failure. 
 
 
9.   NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (4) of section 37 of the 
Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994), the Tamil Nadu State Election Commission 
hereby declares that the candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below against the contested election 
mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, shall be disqualified, for being chosen as a 
member or president for a period of three years from the date of this Order.

[ELECTIONS – ORDINARY ELECTIONS TO RURAL LOCAL BODIES – OCTOBER 2011 – 
KANCHEEPURAM  DISTRICT – CONTESTED CANDIDATES – ACCOUNTS OF ELECTION 
EXPENSES  - FAILURE TO LODGE - SHOW CAUSE NOTICES ISSUED – FAILED TO 
SUBMIT EXPLANATION AND ACCOUNTS - DISQUALIFICATION – ORDERED.] 
 
(S.O.No.40/2013/TNSEC/PE-2.)                         
 
NO. VI (2)/213(b-4) /2013. 
 
 
 
WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. first read above, by invoking sub-rule (3) of the 
rule 120 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats (Elections) Rules, 1995, the Commission directed that all the 
contesting candidates in the elections listed therein shall lodge a true copy of their election expenses kept by 
them or by their respective election agent under sub-rule (1) of rule 120 of the said Rules in the format 
prescribed therefor under sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules with the officers mentioned therein, 
within thirty days from the date of declaration of the result of the elections; 
 
 
2. WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. second read above, this Commission 
prescribed a format for the said purpose by invoking sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules; 
 
 
3.  WHEREAS, this Commission conducted Ordinary Elections to the Rural Local Bodies during 
October 2011;   


 
 
                       TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY                  175
 
4.  WHEREAS, the District Election Officer/District Collector, Kancheepuram, in the letter third read 
above reported that 1330 candidates contested in the said Ordinary Elections for various offices  failed to 
lodge copies of their account of election expenses as directed by this Commission; 
 
 
5. WHEREAS, based on the report of the said District Election Officer/District Collector, a show 
cause notice was issued   in the reference fourth read above to each of  1330 contested candidate who failed 
to lodge a true copy of the account of election expenses in the Ordinary Elections held during the month of 
October, 2011, through the District Election Officer/District Collector, calling for explanation within 20 days of 
the receipt of the said Notice, as to why action should not be taken against him/her as per sub-section (4) of 
section 37 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994); 
 
6.  WHEREAS, on receipt of show cause notices 13 number of candidates have submitted their 
account directly to the Commission and the same have been forwarded to District Election Officer in the 
reference sixth cited and requested to send his remarks along with the reports of other candidates. 
 
 
7. WHEREAS, the said District Election Officer/District Collector, in his letter seventh read above, 
has now reported that out of the said 1330 contested candidates two candidates expired, 1162 contested 
candidates have submitted their accounts and the explanation and the remaining 166 contested candidates 
have neither submitted their explanations nor lodged the account of election expenses in spite of the show 
cause notices issued to them; and 
 
 
8. WHEREAS, in view of the said report of the District Election Officer/District Collector, the           
Tamil Nadu State Election Commission is satisfied that 166 candidates listed in column (3) of the Table 
below against the contested election mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, have failed 
to lodge an account of election expenses as required by or under the said Act and have no justification for 
the failure. 
 
 
9.  NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (4) of section 37 of the 
Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994), the Tamil Nadu State Election Commission 
hereby declares that the candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below against the contested election 
mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, shall be disqualified, for being chosen as a 
member or president for a period of three years from the date of this Order.

                       TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY                  189
 
[ELECTIONS – ORDINARY ELECTIONS TO RURAL LOCAL BODIES – OCTOBER 2011 – SIVANGANGA  
DISTRICT – CONTESTED CANDIDATES – ACCOUNTS OF ELECTION EXPENSES  - FAILURE TO 
LODGE - SHOW CAUSE NOTICES ISSUED – FAILED TO SUBMIT EXPLANATION AND ACCOUNTS 
- DISQUALIFICATION – ORDERED.] 
 
(S.O.No.41/2013/TNSEC/PE-2.) 
No. VI (2)/213(b-5) /2013. 
 
WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. first read above, by invoking sub-rule (3) of the 
rule 120 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats (Elections) Rules, 1995, the Commission directed that all the 
contesting candidates in the elections listed therein shall lodge a true copy of their election expenses kept by 
them or by their respective election agent under sub-rule (1) of rule 120 of the said Rules in the format 
prescribed therefor under sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules with the officers mentioned therein, 
within thirty days from the date of declaration of the result of the elections; 
 
 
 
2.  WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. second read above, this Commission 
prescribed a format for the said purpose by invoking sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules; 
 
 
3.  WHEREAS, this Commission conducted Ordinary Elections to the Rural Local Bodies during 
October 2011; 
 
 
4.  WHEREAS, the District Election Officer/District Collector, Sivaganga, in the letter third read 
above reported that 486 candidates contested in the said Ordinary Elections for various offices  failed to 
lodge copies of their account of election expenses as directed by this Commission; 
 
 
5.  WHEREAS, based on the report of the said District Election Officer/District Collector, a show 
cause notice was issued   in the reference fourth read above to each of the contested candidate who failed to 
lodge a true copy of the account of election expenses in the Ordinary Elections held during the month of 
October, 2011, through the District Election Officer/District Collector, calling for explanation within 20 days of 
the receipt of the said Notice, as to why action should not be taken against him/her as per sub-section (4) of 
section 37 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994); 
 
6.  WHEREAS, on receipt of show cause notices 38 number of candidates have submitted their 
account directly to the Commission and the same have been forwarded to District Election Officer in the 
reference fifth cited and requested to send his remarks along with the reports of other candidates. 
 
 
7.  WHEREAS, the said District Election Officer/District Collector, in his letter seventh read above, 
has now reported that out of the said 486 contested candidates two of them have expired, 155 contested 
candidates have submitted their explanation along with the accounts within the time prescibed and 329 
contested candidates, have neither submitted their explanations nor lodged the account of election expenses 
in spite of the show cause notices issued to them; and 
 
 
8.  WHEREAS, in view of the said report of the District Election Officer/District Collector, the Tamil 
Nadu State Election Commission is satisfied that 329 candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below 
against the contested election mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, have failed to 
lodge an account of election expenses as required by or under the said Act and have no justification for the 
failure. 
 
 
9.  NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (4) of section 37 of the 
Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994), the Tamil Nadu State Election Commission 
hereby declares that the candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below against the contested election 
mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, shall be disqualified, for being chosen as a 
member or president for a period of three years from the date of this Order. 
 
 
 
 
 
 


                      TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY

[ELECTIONS – ORDINARY ELECTIONS TO RURAL LOCAL BODIES – OCTOBER 2011 – 
TIRUVANNAMALAI DISTRICT – CONTESTED CANDIDATES – ACCOUNTS OF ELECTION 
EXPENSES - FAILURE TO LODGE - SHOW CAUSE NOTICES ISSUED – FAILED TO 
SUBMIT EXPLANATION AND ACCOUNTS - DISQUALIFICATION – ORDERED.] 
 
(S.O.No.42/2013/TNSEC/PE-2.)  
 
NO. VI (2)/213(b-6) /2013. 
 
 
WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. first read above, by invoking sub-rule (3) of the 
rule 120 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats (Elections) Rules, 1995, the Commission directed that all the 
contesting candidates in the elections listed therein shall lodge a true copy of their election expenses kept by 
them or by their respective election agent under sub-rule (1) of rule 120 of the said Rules in the format 
prescribed therefor under sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules with the officers mentioned therein, 
within thirty days from the date of declaration of the result of the elections; 
 
 
2.   WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. second read above, this Commission 
prescribed a format for the said purpose by invoking sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules; 
 
 
3.   WHEREAS, this Commission conducted Ordinary Elections to the Rural Local Bodies during 
October 2011; 
 
 
4. WHEREAS, the District Election Officer/District Collector, Tiruvannamalai, in the letter third read 
above reported that 2018 candidates contested in the said Ordinary Elections for various offices  failed to 
lodge copies of their account of election expenses as directed by this Commission; 
 
 
5.  WHEREAS, based on the report of the said District Election Officer/District Collector,  a  show 
cause notice  was issued   in the reference fourth read above to each of the contested candidate who failed 
to lodge a true copy of the account of election expenses in the Ordinary Elections held during the month of 
October, 2011, through the District Election Officer/District Collector, calling for explanation within 20 days of 


                      TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
208 
the receipt of the said Notice, as to why action should not be taken against him/her as per sub-section (4) of 
Section 37 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994); 
 
6.    WHEREAS, on receipt of show cause notices 74 candidates have submitted their account 
directly to the Commission and the same have been forwarded to District Election Officer in the reference 
sixth cited and requested to send his remarks along with the reports of other candidates. 
 
 
7.   WHEREAS, the said District Election Officer/District Collector, in his letter seventh read above, 
has now reported that out of the said 2018 contested candidates,  6 candidates have expired, 543 contested 
candidates have submitted their accounts along with the explanation and 1469 contested candidates, have 
neither submitted their explanations nor lodged the account of election expenses in spite of the show cause 
notices issued to them; and 
 
 
8.  WHEREAS, in view of the said report of the District Election Officer/District Collector, the  
Tamil Nadu State Election Commission is satisfied that 1469 candidates listed in column (3) of the Table 
below against the contested election mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, have failed 
to lodge an account of election expenses as required by or under the said Act and have no justification for 
the failure. 
 
 
9.    NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (4) of Section 37 of the 
Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994), the Tamil Nadu State Election Commission 
hereby declares that the candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below against the contested election 
mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, shall be disqualified, for being chosen as a 
member or president for a period of three years from the date of this Order. 
 
THE TABLE 
 
 TIRUVANNAMALAI DISTRICT

(2)

                      TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
310 
[ELECTIONS – ORDINARY ELECTIONS TO RURAL LOCAL BODIES – OCTOBER 2011 – 
SALEM  DISTRICT – CONTESTED CANDIDATES – ACCOUNTS OF ELECTION EXPENSES  
- FAILURE TO LODGE - SHOW CAUSE NOTICES ISSUED – FAILED TO SUBMIT 
EXPLANATION AND ACCOUNTS - DISQUALIFICATION – ORDERED.] 
 
(S.O.No.43/2013/TNSEC/PE-2.)  
 
NO. VI (2)/213 (b-7)/2013. 
 
WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. first read above, by invoking sub-rule (3) of the 
rule 120 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats (Elections) Rules, 1995, the Commission directed that all the 
contesting candidates in the elections listed therein shall lodge a true copy of their election expenses kept by 
them or by their respective election agent under sub-rule (1) of rule 120 of the said Rules in the format 
prescribed therefor under sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules with the officers mentioned therein, 
within thirty days from the date of declaration of the result of the elections;  
 
2.  WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. second read above, this Commission 
prescribed a format for the said purpose by invoking sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules; 
 
 
 
3.  WHEREAS, this Commission conducted Ordinary Elections to the Rural Local Bodies during 
October 2011; 
 
 
4.  WHEREAS, the District Election Officer/District Collector, Salem, in the letter third read above 
reported that 1098 candidates contested in the said Ordinary Elections for various offices  failed to lodge 
copies of their account of election expenses as directed by this Commission; 
 
 
5.  WHEREAS, based on the report of the said District Election Officer/District Collector, a show 
cause notice was issued   in the reference fourth read above to each of the contested candidate who failed to 
lodge a true copy of the account of election expenses in the Ordinary Elections held during the month of 
October, 2011, through the District Election Officer/District Collector, calling for explanation within 20 days of 
the receipt of the said Notice, as to why action should not be taken against him/her as per sub-section (4) of 
section 37 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994); 
 
6.  WHEREAS, on receipt of show cause notices 37 candidates have submitted their account directly 
to the Commission and the same have been forwarded to District Election Officer in the reference sixth cited 
and requested to send his remarks along with the reports of other candidates. 
 
 
7.  WHEREAS, the said District Election Officer/District Collector, in his letter seventh read above, 
has now reported that out of the said 1098 contested candidates thirteen candidates have expired, 225 
contested candidates have submitted their explanation along with the accounts within the time prescibed and 
860 contested candidates, have neither submitted their explanations nor lodged the account of election 
expenses in spite of the show cause notices issued to them; and 
 
 
8.  WHEREAS, in view of the said report of the District Election Officer/District Collector, the Tamil 
Nadu State Election Commission is satisfied that 860 candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below 
against the contested election mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, have failed to 
lodge an account of election expenses as required by or under the said Act and have no justification for the 
failure. 
 
 
9.  NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (4) of section 37 of the 
Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994), the Tamil Nadu State Election Commission 
hereby declares that the candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below against the contested election 
mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, shall be disqualified, for being chosen as a 
member or president for a period of three years from the date of this Order. 
 
 
 
 
 
 


 
 
                       TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY                   311

                      TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY 
 
390 
 
 
 
[ELECTIONS – ORDINARY ELECTIONS TO RURAL LOCAL BODIES – OCTOBER 2011 – 
DINDIGUL DISTRICT – CONTESTED CANDIDATES – ACCOUNTS OF ELECTION 
EXPENSES - FAILURE TO LODGE - SHOW CAUSE NOTICES ISSUED – FAILED TO 
SUBMIT EXPLANATION AND ACCOUNTS - DISQUALIFICATION – ORDERED.] 
 
(S.O.No.44/2013/TNSEC/PE-2.)  
 
NO. VI (2)/213(b-8)/2013. 
 
WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. first read above, by invoking sub-rule (3) of the 
rule 120 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats (Elections) Rules, 1995, the Commission directed that all the 
contesting candidates in the elections listed therein shall lodge a true copy of their election expenses kept by 
them or by their respective election agent under sub-rule (1) of rule 120 of the said Rules in the format 
prescribed therefor under sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules with the officers mentioned therein, 
within thirty days from the date of declaration of the result of the elections; 
 
 
2.  WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. second read above, this Commission 
prescribed a format for the said purpose by invoking sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules; 
 
 
3.  WHEREAS, this Commission conducted Ordinary Elections to the Rural Local Bodies during 
October 2011; 
 
 
4.  WHEREAS, the District Election Officer/District Collector, Dindigul, in the letter third read above 
reported that 748 candidates contested in the said Ordinary Elections for various offices  failed to lodge 
copies of their account of election expenses as directed by this Commission; 
 
 
5.  WHEREAS, based on the report of the said District Election Officer/District Collector, a show 
cause notice was issued  in the reference fourth read above to each of the contested candidate who failed to 
lodge a true copy of the account of election expenses in the Ordinary Elections held during the month of 
October, 2011, through the District Election Officer/District Collector, calling for explanation within 20 days of 
the receipt of the said Notice, as to why action should not be taken against him/her as per sub-section (4) of 
section 37 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994); 
 
855. 
Village Panchayat President 
 Vellakadai Village Panchayat  
Yercaud panchayat Union  
Salem District

S/o.Vellaikumpan, 
Nallur,

                        TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY                 391
 
6.  WHEREAS, on receipt of show cause notices 22 candidates have submitted their account directly 
to the Commission and the same have been forwarded to District Election Officer in the reference sixth cited 
and requested to send his remarks along with the reports of other candidates. 
 
 
7.  WHEREAS, the said District Election Officer/District Collector, in his letter ninth read above, has 
now reported that out of the said 748 contested candidates, four candidates have expired, 121 contested 
candidates have submitted their explanation along with the accounts and 623 contested candidates, have 
neither submitted their explanations nor lodged the account of election expenses in spite of the show cause 
notices issued to them; and 
 
8.  WHEREAS, in view of the said report of the District Election Officer/District Collector, the Tamil 
Nadu State Election Commission is satisfied that 623 candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below 
against the contested election mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, have failed to 
lodge an account of election expenses as required by or under the said Act and have no justification for the 
failure. 
 
 
9.  NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (4) of section 37 of the 
Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994), the Tamil Nadu State Election Commission 
hereby declares that the candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below against the contested election 
mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, shall be disqualified, for being chosen as a 
member or president for a period of three years from the date of this Order.

[ELECTIONS – ORDINARY ELECTIONS TO RURAL LOCAL BODIES – OCTOBER 2011 – 
ARIYALUR DISTRICT – CONTESTED CANDIDATES – ACCOUNTS OF ELECTION 
EXPENSES - FAILURE TO LODGE - SHOW CAUSE NOTICES ISSUED – FAILED TO 
SUBMIT EXPLANATION AND ACCOUNTS - DISQUALIFICATION – ORDERED.] 
 
(S.O.No.45/2013/TNSEC/PE-2.)  
 
NO. VI (2)/213(b-9)/2013. 
 
 
WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. first read above, by invoking sub-rule (3) of the 
rule 120 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats (Elections) Rules, 1995, the Commission directed that all the 
contesting candidates in the elections listed therein shall lodge a true copy of their election expenses kept by 
them or by their respective election agent under sub-rule (1) of rule 120 of the said Rules in the format 
prescribed therefor under sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules with the officers mentioned therein, 
within thirty days from the date of declaration of the result of the elections; 
 
 
2.  WHEREAS, in the Notification issued with the S.O. second read above, this Commission 
prescribed a format for the said purpose by invoking sub-rule (2) of the rule 120 of the said Rules; 
 
3.  WHEREAS, this Commission conducted Ordinary Elections to the Rural Local Bodies during 
October 2011; 
 
4.  WHEREAS, the District Election Officer/District Collector, Ariyalur, in the letter third read above 
reported that 250 candidates contested in the said Ordinary Elections for various offices  failed to lodge 
copies of their account of election expenses as directed by this Commission; 
 
5.  WHEREAS, based on the report of the said District Election Officer/District Collector, show cause 
notices were issued   in the reference fourth read above to each of the contested candidates who failed to 
lodge a true copy of the account of election expenses in the Ordinary Elections held during the month of 
October, 2011, through the District Election Officer/District Collector, calling for explanation within 20 days of 
the receipt of the said Notice, as to why action should not be taken against him/her as per sub-section (4) of 
section 37 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994); 
 
6.  WHEREAS, on receipt of show cause notices 5 number of candidates have submitted their 
accounts directly to the Commission and the same has been forwarded to the District Election Officer in the 
reference sixth cited and informed to send his remarks along with the reports of other candidates.  
 
7.  WHEREAS, the said District Election Officer/District Collector, in his letter ninth read above, has 
now reported that, one candidate Thiru. A.K Appasamy Senthurai Panchayat Union, Unjini Village 
Panchayat, contested for Village Panchayat President Election has submitted his accounts and explanation 
belatedly (49 days) and hence recommended for disqualification. However further report has been called for 
by the Commission from District Election Officer/District Collector Ariyalur, in this regard. The District Election 
Officer/District Collector in his report dated, 18.10.2013 informed that the delay is the only reason for which 
disqualification was recommended early.  
 
However, after careful consideration the Commission has decided to condone the delay in exercise 
of powers conferred under rule 120 (13) of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats (Elections) Rules, 1995. 


 
 
                        TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY                 437
 
 
8.  WHEREAS, in veiw of the  said District Election Officer/District Collector, the Tamil Nadu State 
Election Commission satisfied that out of the said 250 contested candidates,  30 contested candidates have 
submitted their explanation along with the accounts and 7 contested candidates, have submitted their  
accounts of election expenses and the expences were beyond the ceiling prescribed and recommended for 
disqualification of the said 7 candidates who have exceeded the ceiling prescribed as per rule 121 of the 
Tamil Nadu Panchayats  (Elections) Rules, 1995. Further, reported that 213 have neither submitted their 
explanations nor lodged the accounts of election expenses in spite of the show cause notices issued to them 
and recommended for disqualification and ; 
 
9.  WHEREAS, in view of the said report of the District Election Officer/District Collector, the Tamil 
Nadu State Election Commission is satisfied that the said 220 candidates (213 +7) listed in column (3) of the 
Table below against the contested election mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, have 
failed to lodge an account of election expenses as required by or under the said Act and have no justification 
for the failure. 
 
 
10.  NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (4) of section 37 of the 
Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994), the Tamil Nadu State Election Commission 
hereby declares that the candidates listed in column (3) of the Table below against the contested election 
mentioned in the corresponding entry in column (2) thereof, shall be disqualified, for being chosen as a 
member or president for a period of three years from the date of this Order. 
 
  
THE TABLE 
 
ARIYALUR DISTRICT
